(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))

    (at ?loc - location)

      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (problem explore-corridor)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects 
    kitchen pantry bathroom living_room backyard - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init 
    (at living_room)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored bathroom)
    (explored living_room)
    (explored backyard)
    (door-between kitchen pantry south)
    (door-between pantry kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen pantry south)
    (door-open pantry kitchen north)
    (door-between kitchen bathroom east)
    (door-between bathroom kitchen west)
    (door-open kitchen bathroom east)
    (door-open bathroom kitchen west)
    (door-between bathroom living_room north)
    (door-between living_room bathroom south)
    (door-open bathroom living_room north)
    (door-open living_room bathroom south)
    (door-between living_room backyard east)
    (door-between backyard living_room west)
    (door-open living_room backyard east)
    (door-open backyard living_room west)
    (door-between kitchen corridor north)
    (door-between corridor kitchen south)
    (door-closed kitchen corridor north)
    (door-closed corridor kitchen south)
  )
  (:goal (at corridor))
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (problem explore-corridor)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects 
    kitchen pantry bathroom living_room backyard corridor - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init 
    (at kitchen)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored bathroom)
    (explored living_room)
    (explored backyard)
    (door-between kitchen pantry south)
    (door-between pantry kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen pantry south)
    (door-open pantry kitchen north)
    (door-between kitchen bathroom east)
    (door-between bathroom kitchen west)
    (door-open kitchen bathroom east)
    (door-open bathroom kitchen west)
    (door-between bathroom living_room north)
    (door-between living_room bathroom south)
    (door-open bathroom living_room north)
    (door-open living_room bathroom south)
    (door-between living_room backyard east)
    (door-between backyard living_room west)
    (door-open living_room backyard east)
    (door-open backyard living_room west)
    (door-between kitchen corridor north)
    (door-between corridor kitchen south)
    
  )
  (:goal (at corridor))
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

Generated df and pf: 
 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))

Generated df and pf: 
 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

Generated df and pf: 
 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)
